SELECT [a].[Id], [a].[ClinicId], [a].[CreatedAt], [a].[DoctorId], [a].[IsActive], [a].[Notes], [a].[OrganizationId], [a].[PatientId], [a].[Status], [a].[TokenNumber], [a].[Type], [a].[UpdatedAt], [a].[AppointmentDate], [p0].[Id], [p0].[Address], [p0].[BloodGroup], [p0].[CreatedAt], [p0].[DateOfBirth], [p0].[EmergencyContact], [p0].[FirstName], [p0].[Gender], [p0].[IsActive], [p0].[LastName], [p0].[MedicalHistory], [p0].[OrganizationId], [p0].[PatientCode], [p0].[Phone], [p0].[UpdatedAt], [p0].[UserId]
FROM [Appointments] AS [a]
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT [p].[Id], [p].[Address], [p].[BloodGroup], [p].[CreatedAt], [p].[DateOfBirth], [p].[EmergencyContact], [p].[FirstName], [p].[Gender], [p].[IsActive], [p].[LastName], [p].[MedicalHistory], [p].[OrganizationId], [p].[PatientCode], [p].[Phone], [p].[UpdatedAt], [p].[UserId]
    FROM [Patients] AS [p]
) AS [p0] ON [a].[PatientId] = [p0].[Id]
WHERE [a].[Status] = 2 AND [a].[AppointmentDate] = @__today_0 AND [a].[IsActive] = CAST(1 AS bit)
